      <section class="cv-content-section cv-section-1 cv-section-main bg-source-color padding-top-normal padding-bottom-none " data-visibility="all" id="cv-section-1" style="background-color:#e2e2e2;">
       <div class="cv-wrap-wrapper">
        <div>
         <div class="wrap has-clearfix is-false no-sidebar">
          <div class="content-section-detail">
           <div class="cv-user-font">
            <div class="cv-content-row has-clearfix" data-visibility="all">
             <script data-cfasync="false" type="text/javascript">
              var lsjQuery = jQuery;
             </script>
             <script data-cfasync="false" type="text/javascript">

             </script>
             <div class="ls-wp-container" id="layerslider_1_1" style="width:1100px;height:252px;margin:0 auto;margin-bottom: 0px; box-shadow: 0 10px 16px 0 rgba(0,0,0,0.2),0 6px 20px 0 rgba(0,0,0,0.19);">
              <div class="ls-slide" data-ls="transition2d:1;">
               <img alt="MainSlider_IndigReport" class="ls-bg" src="http://www.healthcarecan.ca/wp-content/uploads/2018/05/MainSlider_IndigReport.jpg"/>
               <a class="ls-link" href="http://www.healthcarecan.ca/2018/04/11/bringing-reconciliation-to-healthcare-in-canada-wise-practices-for-healthcare-leaders/" target="_self">
               </a>

             <h2>
              Leading. Innovation. Together.
             </h2>
             <hr/>
             <div class="clearfix">
             </div>

                </div>
                <h3 class="cv-icon-box-title">
                 Advancing S&amp;T in Service of Health
                </h3>
                <div class="cv-icon-box-content">
                 <p style="text-align: center;">
                  The increasing complexity of health and healthcare demands an ongoing focus on patients, a re-commitment to research and the acceleration of the spread and uptake of research results.
                  <br/>
                  <a href="/what-we-do/research-innovation/">
                   Learn more
                  </a>
                 </p>

              </div>
             </div>
             <div>

                </div>
                <h3 class="cv-icon-box-title">
                 Supporting Service Excellence
                </h3>
                <div class="cv-icon-box-content">

                  <br/>

                   Learn more
                  </a>
                 </p>
                 <div class="clearfix">
